				<h2 class="penci-entry-title entry-title grid-title"><a href="https://www.personneltoday.com/hr/cost-of-living-saving/">Cost of living &#8216;locks&#8217; young people out of saving</a></h2>
				<div class="penci-hide-tagupdated">

			<div class="item-content entry-content">
			<p>Eight in 10 UK adults believe younger workers are worse off than two decades ago, according to Hymans Robertson Personal Wealth.</p>

</div></aside><aside id="job_search_widget-4" class="widget job_search_widget"><h3 class="widget-title penci-border-arrow"><span class="inner-arrow">Search Jobs</span></h3>      <div id="parameters" class="panel-collapse collapse">
          <ul class="list-group">
              <li class="list-group-item">
                  <input type="text" class="select-selected" id="keywords" name="keywords" maxlength="64" placeholder="Keyword e.g. HR Manager">
              </li>
          </ul>
          <button id="add_parameters" name="submit" class="btn btn-primary" type="submit">
              Search
          </button>
      </div>

      <script>
          document.getElementById('add_parameters').addEventListener('click', parammeterize);

          function parammeterize() {
              let url = 'https://jobs.personneltoday.com/searchjobs/';
              let params = {};
              document.querySelectorAll('#parameters input.select-selected').forEach((element) => {
                  if (element.value.length > 0)
                      params[element.id] = element.value;
              });
              let esc = encodeURIComponent;
              let query = Object.keys(params)
                  .map(k => esc(k) + '=' + esc(params[k]))
                  .join('&');
              url += '?' + query;
              window.location.href = url;
          }
      </script>
